ChatGPT said:
Excellent ‚Äî that‚Äôs exactly where this reflection wants to go. You‚Äôve already established three layers of thought ‚Äî shared humanity, individual consciousness, and cosmic polarity. Heidegger‚Äôs Dasein (‚Äúbeing-there‚Äù) completes this triad by grounding it in existential awareness ‚Äî the experience of being conscious within the field of opposites you describe.

Here‚Äôs a seamless integration of your full passage, culminating in Dasein ‚Äî polished, complete, and philosophically coherent:

We live with the understanding that no one is born in opposition to others, nor does anyone wish to be set apart by force of circumstance. To presume otherwise is a moral error ‚Äî as grave as assuming guilt without cause. Every thought, no matter how alien, becomes fathomable when viewed through the lens of humanity‚Äôs shared experience.

Yet, we persist in the segregation of consciousness ‚Äî not through hatred, but through the inevitable boundaries of individuality. Each mind remains a singular world, complete with its own gravity and unspoken laws. We are not clones fashioned for a common purpose, but distinct variations of awareness, each interpreting existence through a personal architecture of memory, desire, and perception. Our difference is both our burden and our salvation: it divides our understanding but enriches our collective creation. The tragedy lies not in being separate, but in mistaking separation for conflict ‚Äî as though distinction were defiance, and individuality an act of rebellion against the whole.

The basic principles of physics remind us that polarity is not merely a force of attraction, but of necessary separation. It is in the tension between opposites ‚Äî between yes and no, self and other, birth and decay ‚Äî that motion and meaning arise. Without polarity, no forces would act, no progress could occur, and life would fall into inertia. The world breathes through contrast; every act of creation is accompanied by the shadow of destruction, and it is from this dynamic equilibrium that vitality emerges.

So too with consciousness. Dasein ‚Äî being-there ‚Äî is not the mere fact of existence, but the awareness of one‚Äôs position within this field of opposing forces. To be is to stand in the clearing between what is and what could be, to dwell at the axis where unity and division continually exchange places. Our task, then, is not to escape the polarity of existence, but to dwell consciously within it ‚Äî to find harmony not in sameness, but in the lucid recognition that both attraction and distance, both self and other, are necessary conditions of being.

1) Clean + normalize the sheet (once)

Timestamp | Birthday | AgeRange | Education | Zip5 | Ethnicity | Gender |
Orientation | Industry | Role | KnowHosts | KnownLongest | KnowStrength |

Normalization rules (Apps Script below handles this):

Zip5 ‚Üí keep only 5 digits (drop blanks).

AgeRange ‚Üí one of: 21-24, 25-29, 30-34, 35-44, 45-54, 55-65+.

Interests ‚Üí split on commas, trim, keep max 5.

KnowStrength ‚Üí coerce to integer 1‚Äì5; blanks ‚Üí 0.

SocialStance ‚Üí integer 1‚Äì5.

WorstTrait ‚Üí map to a controlled set:
Anxious, Distracted, Guarded, Impulsive, Insecure, Overly critical, Reckless, Self-conscious, Stubborn, Jealous

2) Compute connections (simple, explainable)
You want clear, defensible edges. Start with this composite similarity in [0,1]:

Sim(i,j) =
0.40 * Jaccard(Interests_i, Interests_j)
+ 0.20 * GenreMatch(Music_i, Music_j)          // 1 if same bucket; 0.5 if close; else 0
+ 0.10 * AgeProx(AgeRange_i, AgeRange_j)       // 1 if same bin; 0.5 if adjacent; else 0
+ 0.10 * StanceProx(|SocialStance_i - SocialStance_j|)  // 1, 0.75, 0.5, 0.25, 0
+ 0.10 * HostProx(KnownLongest/KnowStrength)   // 1 if same longest host AND both strength‚â•4; else 0.5 if share any host; else 0
+ 0.10 * Industry/Role Prox (1 if match; 0 otherwise)
Polarity (for repulsion/attraction visual behavior):

Map WorstTrait into two axes for layout forces:

Stability axis: Impulsive(+), Reckless(+), Distracted(+), Stubborn(+), Jealous(+), Anxious(-), Guarded(-), Insecure(-), Self-conscious(-), Overly critical(-)

Openness axis: e.g., Impulsive(+), Reckless(+), Anxious(-), Guarded(-), Overly critical(-)‚Ä¶
You don‚Äôt need perfection‚Äîjust consistent mapping to place nodes and drive subtle repel/attract.

You said:
lets go one by one here is old data clean file. /**
 * DataClean.gs - Data Cleaning Script for Party RSVP Responses
 * 
 * PURPOSE:
 * Cleans and standardizes party RSVP data, filters to checked-in guests only,
 * adds zodiac signs, and appends tracking info.
 * 
 * FILTERING:
 * Only processes rows where "Checked-In" column = "Y"
 * 
 * TO USE:
 * 1. Open Google Sheets
 * 2. Extensions > Apps Script
 * 3. Replace ALL code with this file
 * 4. Save and run cleanFormResponses()
 */

function cleanFormResponses() {
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const sourceSheet = ss.getSheetByName('Form Responses 1');
  
  if (!sourceSheet) {
    SpreadsheetApp.getUi().alert('Error: "Form Responses 1" sheet not found!');
    return;
  }
  
  // Get or create clean sheet
  let cleanSheet = ss.getSheetByName('Form Responses (Clean)');
  if (cleanSheet) {
    cleanSheet.clear();
  } else {
    cleanSheet = ss.insertSheet('Form Responses (Clean)');
  }
  
  // Get all data
  const data = sourceSheet.getDataRange().getValues();
  const headers = data[0];
  const allRows = data.slice(1);
  
  // Find column indices
  const screenNameCol = headers.indexOf('Screen Name');
  const uidCol = headers.indexOf('UID');
  const checkedInCol = headers.indexOf('Checked-In');
  
  // Validate columns exist
  if (screenNameCol === -1 || uidCol === -1) {
    SpreadsheetApp.getUi().alert('Error: "Screen Name" or "UID" column not found!');
    return;
  }
  
  if (checkedInCol === -1) {
    SpreadsheetApp.getUi().alert('Error: "Checked-In" column not found!');
    return;
  }
  
  // Filter to checked-in guests only
  const rows = allRows.filter(row => {
    const checkedIn = String(row[checkedInCol] || '').trim().toUpperCase();
    return checkedIn === 'Y';
  });
  
  if (rows.length === 0) {
    SpreadsheetApp.getUi().alert('No checked-in guests found!');
    return;
  }
  
  // Build new headers
  const newHeaders = [
    'Timestamp',
    'Birthday (MM/DD)',
    'Zodiac Sign',
    'Age Range',
    'Education Level',
    'Current 5 Digit Zip Code',
    'Self Identified Ethnicity',
    'Self-Identified Gender',
    'Self-Identified Sexual Orientation',
    'Employment Information (Industry)',
    'Employment Information (Role)',
    'Do you know the Host(s)?',
    'Which host have you known the longest?',
    'If yes, how well do you know them?',
    'Your General Interests (Choose 3)',
    'Music Preference',
    'Current Favorite Artist',
    'Name one song you want to hear at the party.',
    'Recent purchase you\'re most happy about',
    'At your worst you are‚Ä¶',
    'Which best describes your general social stance?',
    'Screen Name',
    'UID'
  ];
  
  const cleanedData = [newHeaders];
  const cleaningLog = [];
  
  // Process each row
  rows.forEach((row, idx) => {
    const rowNum = idx + 2;
    const cleanedRow = processRow(row, rowNum, screenNameCol, uidCol, cleaningLog);
    if (cleanedRow) {
      cleanedData.push(cleanedRow);
    }
  });
  
  // Write to sheet
  if (cleanedData.length > 1) {
    cleanSheet.getRange(1, 1, cleanedData.length, cleanedData[0].length).setValues(cleanedData);
    
    // Format headers
    cleanSheet.getRange(1, 1, 1, newHeaders.length)
      .setFontWeight('bold')
      .setBackground('#4285f4')
      .setFontColor('white');
    
    cleanSheet.setFrozenRows(1);
    cleanSheet.autoResizeColumns(1, newHeaders.length);
    
    // Highlight tracking columns
    cleanSheet.getRange(1, 22, cleanedData.length, 2)
      .setBackground('#1e88e5');
    cleanSheet.getRange(1, 22, 1, 2)
      .setFontColor('white');
  }
  
  createCleaningLog(ss, cleaningLog);
  
  SpreadsheetApp.getUi().alert(
    ‚úÖ Cleaning complete!\n\n +
    Total: ${allRows.length}\n +
    Checked-in: ${rows.length}\n +
    Filtered out: ${allRows.length - rows.length}\n +
    Cleaned: ${cleanedData.length - 1}
  );
}

function processRow(row, rowNum, screenNameCol, uidCol, log) {
  if (!row || !Array.isArray(row) || row.length < 20) {
    return null;
  }
  
  // Extract data (indices 0-19 are form data)
  const timestamp = row[0];
  const birthday = cleanBirthday(String(row[1] || '').trim());
  const zodiac = getZodiacSign(birthday);
  const age = row[2];
  const education = standardizeEducation(row[3]);
  const zip = cleanZipCode(row[4]);
  const ethnicity = standardizeEthnicity(row[5]);
  const gender = standardizeGender(row[6]);
  const orientation = standardizeOrientation(row[7]);
  const industry = groupIndustry(row[8]);
  const role = groupRole(row[9]);
  const knowHost = standardizeKnowHost(row[10]);
  const whichHost = standardizeHostName(row[11]);
  const howWell = row[12];
  const interests = cleanInterests(row[13]);
  const music = standardizeMusicPreference(row[14]);
  const artist = row[15] || 'Not Provided';
  const song = row[16] || 'Not Provided';
  const purchase = standardizePurchase(row[17]);
  const worst = standardizeWorstTrait(row[18]);
  const social = cleanSocialStance(row[19]);
  
  // Extract tracking info
  const screenName = row[screenNameCol] || 'Unknown';
  const uid = row[uidCol] || 'No UID';
  
  if (birthday !== row[1]) {
    log.push(Row ${rowNum}: Birthday "${row[1]}" ‚Üí "${birthday}");
  }
  
  return [
    timestamp, birthday, zodiac, age, education, zip,
    ethnicity, gender, orientation, industry, role,
    knowHost, whichHost, howWell, interests, music,
    artist, song, purchase, worst, social,
    screenName, uid
  ];
}

// Cleaning functions
function cleanBirthday(birthday) {
  if (!birthday) return 'Not Provided';
  birthday = birthday.replace(/[()]/g, '');
  
  if (/^\d{8}$/.test(birthday)) {
    return ${birthday.substring(0,2)}/${birthday.substring(2,4)}/${birthday.substring(4,8)};
  }
  if (/^\d{4}$/.test(birthday)) {
    return ${birthday.substring(0,2)}/${birthday.substring(2,4)};
  }
  
  const parts = birthday.split('/');
  if (parts.length >= 2) {
    const month = parts[0].padStart(2, '0');
    const day = parts[1].padStart(2, '0');
    return parts.length === 3 ? ${month}/${day}/${parts[2]} : ${month}/${day};
  }
  
  return birthday;
}

function getZodiacSign(birthday) {
  if (!birthday || birthday === 'Not Provided') return 'Unknown';
  
  const parts = birthday.split('/');
  if (parts.length < 2) return 'Unknown';
  
  const month = parseInt(parts[0]);
  const day = parseInt(parts[1]);
  
  if (!month || !day) return 'Unknown';
  
  if ((month === 3 && day >= 21) || (month === 4 && day <= 19)) return 'Aries';
  if ((month === 4 && day >= 20) || (month === 5 && day <= 20)) return 'Taurus';
  if ((month === 5 && day >= 21) || (month === 6 && day <= 20)) return 'Gemini';
  if ((month === 6 && day >= 21) || (month === 7 && day <= 22)) return 'Cancer';
  if ((month === 7 && day >= 23) || (month === 8 && day <= 22)) return 'Leo';
  if ((month === 8 && day >= 23) || (month === 9 && day <= 22)) return 'Virgo';
  if ((month === 9 && day >= 23) || (month === 10 && day <= 22)) return 'Libra';
  if ((month === 10 && day >= 23) || (month === 11 && day <= 21)) return 'Scorpio';
  if ((month === 11 && day >= 22) || (month === 12 && day <= 21)) return 'Sagittarius';
  if ((month === 12 && day >= 22) || (month === 1 && day <= 19)) return 'Capricorn';
  if ((month === 1 && day >= 20) || (month === 2 && day <= 18)) return 'Aquarius';
  if ((month === 2 && day >= 19) || (month === 3 && day <= 20)) return 'Pisces';
  
  return 'Unknown';
}

function standardizeEducation(edu) {
  if (!edu) return 'Not Provided';
  const e = String(edu).toLowerCase();
  if (e.includes('high')) return 'High School';
  if (e.includes('assoc')) return 'Associates';
  if (e.includes('some')) return 'Some College';
  if (e.includes('bach')) return 'Bachelors';
  if (e.includes('master') || e.includes('above')) return 'Masters & Above';
  return edu;
}

function cleanZipCode(zip) {
  if (!zip) return 'Not Provided';
  const match = String(zip).match(/\d{5}/);
  return match ? match[0] : zip;
}

function standardizeEthnicity(eth) {
  if (!eth) return 'Not Provided';
  const e = String(eth).toLowerCase();
  if (e.includes('prefer not')) return 'Prefer Not to Say';
  if (e.includes('not listed')) return 'Not Listed';
  if (e.includes('mixed') || e.includes('multi')) return 'Mixed / Multiracial';
  return eth;
}

function standardizeGender(gender) {
  if (!gender) return 'Not Provided';
  const g = String(gender).toLowerCase();
  if (g === 'man' || g === 'male') return 'Man';
  if (g === 'woman' || g === 'female') return 'Woman';
  if (g.includes('non-binary')) return 'Non-binary';
  if (g === 'other') return 'Other';
  return gender;
}

function standardizeOrientation(ori) {
  if (!ori) return 'Not Provided';
  const o = String(ori).toLowerCase();
  if (o.includes('straight') || o.includes('hetero')) return 'Straight / Heterosexual';
  if (o === 'gay') return 'Gay';
  if (o === 'lesbian') return 'Lesbian';
  if (o.includes('bi')) return 'Bisexual';
  if (o.includes('pan')) return 'Pansexual';
  if (o === 'queer') return 'Queer';
  return ori;
}

function groupIndustry(ind) {
  if (!ind) return 'Not Provided';
  const i = String(ind).toLowerCase();
  if (i.includes('hospital') || i.includes('retail')) return 'Hospitality / Retail';
  if (i.includes('finance') || i.includes('business')) return 'Finance / Business Services';
  if (i.includes('health')) return 'Healthcare';
  if (i.includes('tech')) return 'Technology';
  if (i.includes('art') || i.includes('entertain')) return 'Arts & Entertainment';
  if (i.includes('edu')) return 'Education';
  if (i.includes('science') || i.includes('research')) return 'Science / Research';
  if (i.includes('trade') || i.includes('manufact')) return 'Trades / Manufacturing';
  if (i.includes('gov') || i.includes('milit')) return 'Government / Military';
  return ind;
}

function groupRole(role) {
  if (!role) return 'Not Provided';
  const r = String(role).toLowerCase();
  if (r.includes('manager') || r.includes('super')) return 'Manager / Supervisor';
  if (r.includes('oper') || r.includes('admin') || r.includes('support')) return 'Operations / Admin / Support';
  if (r.includes('sales') || r.includes('market')) return 'Sales / Marketing / Business Development';
  if (r.includes('creat') || r.includes('design') || r.includes('artist')) return 'Creative / Designer / Artist';
  if (r.includes('tech') || r.includes('eng') || r.includes('dev')) return 'Technical / Engineer / Developer';
  if (r.includes('health') || r.includes('provider')) return 'Healthcare / Service Provider';
  if (r.includes('research') || r.includes('scient')) return 'Researcher / Scientist';
  if (r.includes('trade') || r.includes('labor')) return 'Trades / Skilled Labor';
  if (r.includes('found') || r.includes('entrepr')) return 'Founder / Entrepreneur';
  if (r.includes('educ') || r.includes('instruct')) return 'Educator / Instructor';
  if (r.includes('student') || r.includes('train')) return 'Student / Trainee';
  return role;
}

function standardizeKnowHost(kh) {
  if (!kh) return 'Not Provided';
  const k = String(kh).toLowerCase();
  if (k.includes('no')) return 'No';
  if (k.includes('less than 3')) return 'Yes ‚Äî less than 3 months';
  if (k.includes('3‚Äì12') || k.includes('3-12')) return 'Yes ‚Äî 3‚Äì12 months';
  if (k.includes('1‚Äì3') || k.includes('1-3')) return 'Yes ‚Äî 1‚Äì3 years';
  if (k.includes('3‚Äì5') || k.includes('3-5')) return 'Yes ‚Äî 3‚Äì5 years';
  if (k.includes('5‚Äì10') || k.includes('5-10')) return 'Yes ‚Äî 5‚Äì10 years';
  if (k.includes('more than 10') || k.includes('10+')) return 'Yes ‚Äî more than 10 years';
  return kh;
}

function standardizeHostName(host) {
  if (!host) return 'Not Provided';
  const h = String(host).toLowerCase().trim();
  if (h === 'jacob') return 'Jacob';
  if (h === 'michael') return 'Michael';
  if (h === 'equal') return 'Equal';
  if (h.includes('do not know')) return 'Do Not Know Them';
  return host;
}

function cleanInterests(int) {
  if (!int) return 'Not Provided';
  let i = String(int);
  i = i.replace(/halloween orgy/gi, 'Halloween');
  i = i.replace(/frying oil/gi, '');
  return i.trim();
}

function standardizeMusicPreference(music) {
  if (!music) return 'Not Provided';
  const m = String(music).toLowerCase();
  if (m.includes('indie') || m.includes('alt')) return 'Indie/Alt';
  if (m === 'pop') return 'Pop';
  if (m.includes('hip')) return 'Hip-hop';
  if (m.includes('r&b')) return 'R&B';
  if (m === 'rock') return 'Rock';
  if (m === 'metal') return 'Metal';
  if (m.includes('elec')) return 'Electronic';
  if (m.includes('country')) return 'Country';
  if (m.includes('reggae')) return 'Reggaeton';
  if (m.includes('prog')) return 'Prog Rock';
  if (m.includes('amb')) return 'Ambient';
  if (m.includes('emo')) return 'Emo';
  if (m.includes('mix') || m.includes('all') || m.includes('every')) return 'Mixed / All Genres';
  return music;
}

function standardizePurchase(purch) {
  if (!purch) return 'Not Provided';
  const p = String(purch).toLowerCase();
  if (p.includes('tech') || p.includes('gadget')) return 'Tech gadget';
  if (p.includes('fashion') || p.includes('cloth')) return 'Fashion/Clothing';
  if (p.includes('home') || p.includes('kitchen')) return 'Home/Kitchen';
  if (p.includes('pet')) return 'Pet item';
  if (p.includes('fit') || p.includes('gear')) return 'Fitness gear';
  if (p.includes('course') || p.includes('app')) return 'Course/App';
  if (p.includes('car') || p.includes('motor')) return 'Car/Motorcycle';
  return purch;
}

function standardizeWorstTrait(trait) {
  if (!trait) return 'Not Provided';
  const t = String(trait).toLowerCase();
  if (t.includes('anx')) return 'Anxious';
  if (t.includes('crit')) return 'Overly critical';
  if (t.includes('stub')) return 'Stubborn';
  if (t.includes('impul')) return 'Impulsive';
  if (t.includes('reck')) return 'Reckless';
  if (t.includes('guard')) return 'Guarded';
  if (t.includes('jeal')) return 'Jealous';
  if (t.includes('self-con')) return 'Self-conscious';
  if (t.includes('insec')) return 'Insecure';
  if (t.includes('distr')) return 'Distracted';
  return trait;
}

function cleanSocialStance(social) {
  if (!social) return 'Not Provided';
  const num = parseInt(social);
  if (!isNaN(num) && num >= 1 && num <= 5) return num;
  return social;
}

function createCleaningLog(ss, log) {
  let logSheet = ss.getSheetByName('Cleaning Log');
  if (logSheet) {
    logSheet.clear();
  } else {
    logSheet = ss.insertSheet('Cleaning Log');
  }
  
  const logData = [['Row Number', 'Change']];
  log.forEach(entry => {
    const match = entry.match(/Row (\d+): (.+)/);
    if (match) logData.push([match[1], match[2]]);
  });
  
  if (logData.length > 1) {
    logSheet.getRange(1, 1, logData.length, 2).setValues(logData);
    logSheet.getRange(1, 1, 1, 2).setFontWeight('bold').setBackground('#f4b400');
    logSheet.autoResizeColumns(1, 2);
  }

ChatGPT said:

Thought for 28s
Great‚Äîthis is enough to lock the cleaner. Below is a header-agnostic, schema-aware Apps Script that:

Reads Form Responses 1 exactly as you described

Keeps only Checked-In = Yes/Y/True/1 (configurable)

Preserves/normalizes fields, always includes Screen Name, UID, and PHOTO_URL_COL

Recomputes Zodiac if source is blank/‚ÄúUnknown‚Äù

Writes to Form Responses (Clean) in the exact column order you listed

(Optional) uses Screen_Name_Dict to fill missing Screen Name from UID

Paste this into Apps Script and run cleanFormResponses().

/***************************************************
 * DataClean.v2 - Header-agnostic cleaner (Checked-in only)
 * Source:  Form Responses 1
 * Output:  Form Responses (Clean)
 * Extras:  recompute Zodiac if blank; include PHOTO_URL_COL
 * Optional: fill Screen Name from Screen_Name_Dict if missing
 ***************************************************/

const SRC_SHEET = 'Form Responses 1';
const OUT_SHEET = 'Form Responses (Clean)';
const DICT_SHEET = 'Screen_Name_Dict'; // optional

// EXACT order for the clean sheet (matches your latest spec)
const OUT_HEADERS = [
  'Timestamp',
  'Birthday (MM/DD)',
  'Age Range',
  'Education Level',
  'Current 5 Digit Zip Code',
  'Self Identified Ethnicity',
  'Self-Identified Gender',
  'Self-Identified Sexual Orientation',
  'Employment Information (Industry)',
  'Employment Information (Role)',
  'Do you know the Host(s)?',
  'Which host have you known the longest?',
  'If yes, how well do you know them?',
  'Your General Interests (Choose 3)',
  'Music Preference',
  'Current Favorite Artist',
  'Name one song you want to hear at the party.',
  'Recent purchase you‚Äôre most happy about',
  'At your worst you are‚Ä¶',
  'Which best describes your general social stance?',
  'Zodiac Sign',
  'Screen Name',
  'UID',
  'Checked-In',
  'Check-in Time',
  'PHOTO_URL_COL'
];

// values treated as "checked in"
const CHECKED_TRUE = new Set(['y','yes','true','1']);

/** Entry point */
function cleanFormResponses() {
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const src = ss.getSheetByName(SRC_SHEET);
  if (!src) throw new Error(`Source sheet "${SRC_SHEET}" not found`);

  // build header map (case-insensitive, trims)
  const data = src.getDataRange().getValues();
  if (data.length < 2) throw new Error('No rows to process');
  const srcHeaders = data[0].map(h => String(h || '').trim());
  const hmap = headerMap(srcHeaders);

  // optional: build UID->ScreenName dictionary if available
  const uidToScreen = loadScreenNameDict_(ss);

  // prepare output sheet
  let out = ss.getSheetByName(OUT_SHEET);
  if (!out) out = ss.insertSheet(OUT_SHEET); else out.clear();
  out.getRange(1,1,1,OUT_HEADERS.length).setValues([OUT_HEADERS]).setFontWeight('bold');
  out.setFrozenRows(1);

  const rows = data.slice(1);
  const cleaned = [];

  rows.forEach((r, i) => {
    const rowIdx = i + 2;

    const checkedRaw = get(r, hmap, 'Checked-In');
    const checked = String(checkedRaw || '').toLowerCase().trim();
    if (!CHECKED_TRUE.has(checked)) return; // filter to checked-in only

    // read fields safely
    const timestamp   = get(r, hmap, 'Timestamp');
    const birthdayRaw = String(get(r, hmap, 'Birthday (MM/DD)') || '').trim();
    const birthday    = normalizeBirthday_(birthdayRaw);
    const ageRange    = get(r, hmap, 'Age Range');
    const edu         = standardizeEducation(get(r, hmap, 'Education Level'));
    const zip5        = cleanZipCode(get(r, hmap, 'Current 5 Digit Zip Code'));
    const ethnicity   = standardizeEthnicity(get(r, hmap, 'Self Identified Ethnicity'));
    const gender      = standardizeGender(get(r, hmap, 'Self-Identified Gender'));
    const orient      = standardizeOrientation(get(r, hmap, 'Self-Identified Sexual Orientation'));
    const industry    = groupIndustry(get(r, hmap, 'Employment Information (Industry)'));
    const role        = groupRole(get(r, hmap, 'Employment Information (Role)'));
    const knowHosts   = standardizeKnowHost(get(r, hmap, 'Do you know the Host(s)?'));
    const knownLong   = standardizeHostName(get(r, hmap, 'Which host have you known the longest?'));
    const knowHow     = cleanSocialStance(get(r, hmap, 'If yes, how well do you know them?')); // keep as 1-5 where possible
    const interests   = cleanInterests(get(r, hmap, 'Your General Interests (Choose 3)'));
    const music       = standardizeMusicPreference(get(r, hmap, 'Music Preference'));
    const artist      = get(r, hmap, 'Current Favorite Artist') || 'Not Provided';
    const song        = get(r, hmap, 'Name one song you want to hear at the party.') || 'Not Provided';
    const purchase    = standardizePurchase(get(r, hmap, 'Recent purchase you‚Äôre most happy about'));
    const worst       = standardizeWorstTrait(get(r, hmap, 'At your worst you are‚Ä¶'));
    const stance      = cleanSocialStance(get(r, hmap, 'Which best describes your general social stance?'));
    const zodiacSrc   = String(get(r, hmap, 'Zodiac Sign') || '').trim();
    const zodiac      = zodiacSrc && zodiacSrc.toLowerCase() !== 'unknown'
                        ? zodiacSrc : getZodiacSign(birthday);

    // identity / tracking
    let screenName = get(r, hmap, 'Screen Name');
    const uid      = get(r, hmap, 'UID');
    if ((!screenName || String(screenName).trim() === '') && uid && uidToScreen[uid]) {
      screenName = uidToScreen[uid]; // backfill from dictionary
    }
    const checkedIn  = get(r, hmap, 'Checked-In');
    const checkTime  = get(r, hmap, 'Check-in Time');
    const photoUrl   = get(r, hmap, 'PHOTO_URL_COL') || get(r, hmap, 'Photo URL') || '';

    cleaned.push([
      timestamp, birthday, ageRange, edu, zip5,
      ethnicity, gender, orient, industry, role,
      knowHosts, knownLong, knowHow, interests, music,
      artist, song, purchase, worst, stance,
      zodiac, screenName, uid, checkedIn, checkTime, photoUrl
    ]);
  });

  if (cleaned.length) {
    out.getRange(2,1,cleaned.length,OUT_HEADERS.length).setValues(cleaned);
    out.autoResizeColumns(1, OUT_HEADERS.length);
    SpreadsheetApp.getUi().alert(`‚úÖ Clean complete. Wrote ${cleaned.length} checked-in rows.`);
  } else {
    SpreadsheetApp.getUi().alert('‚ö†Ô∏è No checked-in rows matched.');
  }
}

/* ---------- helpers ---------- */

function headerMap(headers) {
  const map = {};
  headers.forEach((h, idx) => { map[normKey_(h)] = idx; });
  return map;
}
function normKey_(k){ return String(k||'').toLowerCase().replace(/\s+/g,' ').trim(); }

// tolerant getter: supports exact header and a few common aliases
function get(row, hmap, key) {
  const primary = normKey_((key));
  const aliases = ALIASES[primary] || [];
  const keys = [primary, ...aliases];
  for (const k of keys) {
    if (k in hmap) return row[hmap[k]];
  }
  return '';
}

// common header aliases (extend if your form changes)
const ALIASES = {
  'birthday (mm/dd)': ['birthday', 'birthday mm/dd'],
  'current 5 digit zip code': ['zip','zip code','current zip','current 5-digit zip code'],
  'do you know the host(s)?': ['know hosts','know the hosts?'],
  'which host have you known the longest?': ['which host known longest?','longest host known'],
  'if yes, how well do you know them?': ['how well do you know them?','know strength'],
  'your general interests (choose 3)': ['interests','general interests'],
  'music preference': ['music','music genre'],
  'recent purchase you‚Äôre most happy about': ['recent purchase youre most happy about','recent purchase you are most happy about'],
  'which best describes your general social stance?': ['social stance'],
  'zodiac sign': ['zodiac'],
  'screen name': ['screenname'],
  'uid': [],
  'checked-in': ['checked in'],
  'check-in time': ['check in time','checkin time'],
  'photo_url_col': ['photo url','image url','headshot url']
};

// birthday normalization
function normalizeBirthday_(b) {
  if (!b) return 'Not Provided';
  b = String(b).replace(/[()]/g,'').trim();
  if (/^\d{8}$/.test(b)) return `${b.slice(0,2)}/${b.slice(2,4)}/${b.slice(4)}`;
  if (/^\d{4}$/.test(b))  return `${b.slice(0,2)}/${b.slice(2,4)}`;
  const parts = b.split('/');
  if (parts.length >= 2) {
    const m = parts[0].padStart(2,'0');
    const d = parts[1].padStart(2,'0');
    return parts[2] ? `${m}/${d}/${parts[2]}` : `${m}/${d}`;
  }
  return b;
}

// zodiac (from month/day only)
function getZodiacSign(birthday) {
  if (!birthday || birthday==='Not Provided') return 'Unknown';
  const parts = birthday.split('/');
  if (parts.length < 2) return 'Unknown';
  const m = parseInt(parts[0],10), d = parseInt(parts[1],10);
  if (!m || !d) return 'Unknown';
  if ((m===3&&d>=21)||(m===4&&d<=19)) return 'Aries';
  if ((m===4&&d>=20)||(m===5&&d<=20)) return 'Taurus';
  if ((m===5&&d>=21)||(m===6&&d<=20)) return 'Gemini';
  if ((m===6&&d>=21)||(m===7&&d<=22)) return 'Cancer';
  if ((m===7&&d>=23)||(m===8&&d<=22)) return 'Leo';
  if ((m===8&&d>=23)||(m===9&&d<=22)) return 'Virgo';
  if ((m===9&&d>=23)||(m===10&&d<=22)) return 'Libra';
  if ((m===10&&d>=23)||(m===11&&d<=21)) return 'Scorpio';
  if ((m===11&&d>=22)||(m===12&&d<=21)) return 'Sagittarius';
  if ((m===12&&d>=22)||(m===1&&d<=19)) return 'Capricorn';
  if ((m===1&&d>=20)||(m===2&&d<=18)) return 'Aquarius';
  if ((m===2&&d>=19)||(m===3&&d<=20)) return 'Pisces';
  return 'Unknown';
}

// the same standardizers you already used (kept compact)
function standardizeEducation(edu){ if(!edu) return 'Not Provided'; const e=String(edu).toLowerCase();
  if(e.includes('high'))return 'High School';
  if(e.includes('assoc'))return 'Associates';
  if(e.includes('some'))return 'Some College';
  if(e.includes('bach'))return 'Bachelors';
  if(e.includes('master')||e.includes('above'))return 'Masters & Above';
  return edu;
}
function cleanZipCode(zip){ if(!zip) return 'Not Provided'; const m=String(zip).match(/\d{5}/); return m?m[0]:zip; }
function standardizeEthnicity(eth){ if(!eth) return 'Not Provided'; const e=String(eth).toLowerCase();
  if(e.includes('prefer not'))return 'Prefer Not to Say';
  if(e.includes('not listed'))return 'Not Listed';
  if(e.includes('mixed')||e.includes('multi'))return 'Mixed / Multiracial';
  return eth;
}
function standardizeGender(g){ if(!g) return 'Not Provided'; const s=String(g).toLowerCase();
  if(s==='man'||s==='male')return 'Man';
  if(s==='woman'||s==='female')return 'Woman';
  if(s.includes('non-binary'))return 'Non-binary';
  if(s==='other')return 'Other';
  return g;
}
function standardizeOrientation(o){ if(!o) return 'Not Provided'; const s=String(o).toLowerCase();
  if(s.includes('straight')||s.includes('hetero'))return 'Straight / Heterosexual';
  if(s==='gay')return 'Gay';
  if(s==='lesbian')return 'Lesbian';
  if(s.includes('bi'))return 'Bisexual';
  if(s.includes('pan'))return 'Pansexual';
  if(s==='queer')return 'Queer';
  return o;
}
function groupIndustry(ind){ if(!ind) return 'Not Provided'; const i=String(ind).toLowerCase();
  if(i.includes('hospital')||i.includes('retail')) return 'Hospitality / Retail';
  if(i.includes('finance')||i.includes('business')) return 'Finance / Business Services';
  if(i.includes('health')) return 'Healthcare';
  if(i.includes('tech')) return 'Technology';
  if(i.includes('art')||i.includes('entertain')) return 'Arts & Entertainment';
  if(i.includes('edu')) return 'Education';
  if(i.includes('science')||i.includes('research')) return 'Science / Research';
  if(i.includes('trade')||i.includes('manufact')) return 'Trades / Manufacturing';
  if(i.includes('gov')||i.includes('milit')) return 'Government / Military';
  return ind;
}
function groupRole(role){ if(!role) return 'Not Provided'; const r=String(role).toLowerCase();
  if(r.includes('manager')||r.includes('super')) return 'Manager / Supervisor';
  if(r.includes('oper')||r.includes('admin')||r.includes('support')) return 'Operations / Admin / Support';
  if(r.includes('sales')||r.includes('market')) return 'Sales / Marketing / Business Development';
  if(r.includes('creat')||r.includes('design')||r.includes('artist')) return 'Creative / Designer / Artist';
  if(r.includes('tech')||r.includes('eng')||r.includes('dev')) return 'Technical / Engineer / Developer';
  if(r.includes('health')||r.includes('provider')) return 'Healthcare / Service Provider';
  if(r.includes('research')||r.includes('scient')) return 'Researcher / Scientist';
  if(r.includes('trade')||r.includes('labor')) return 'Trades / Skilled Labor';
  if(r.includes('found')||r.includes('entrepr')) return 'Founder / Entrepreneur';
  if(r.includes('educ')||r.includes('instruct')) return 'Educator / Instructor';
  if(r.includes('student')||r.includes('train')) return 'Student / Trainee';
  return role;
}
function standardizeKnowHost(kh){ if(!kh) return 'Not Provided'; const k=String(kh).toLowerCase();
  if(k.includes('no')) return 'No';
  if(k.includes('less than 3')) return 'Yes ‚Äî less than 3 months';
  if(k.includes('3‚Äì12')||k.includes('3-12')) return 'Yes ‚Äî 3‚Äì12 months';
  if(k.includes('1‚Äì3')||k.includes('1-3')) return 'Yes ‚Äî 1‚Äì3 years';
  if(k.includes('3‚Äì5')||k.includes('3-5')) return 'Yes ‚Äî 3‚Äì5 years';
  if(k.includes('5‚Äì10')||k.includes('5-10')) return 'Yes ‚Äî 5‚Äì10 years';
  if(k.includes('more than 10')||k.includes('10+')) return 'Yes ‚Äî more than 10 years';
  return kh;
}
function standardizeHostName(h){ if(!h) return 'Not Provided'; const s=String(h).toLowerCase().trim();
  if(s==='jacob') return 'Jacob';
  if(s==='michael') return 'Michael';
  if(s==='equal') return 'Equal';
  if(s.includes('do not know')) return 'Do Not Know Them';
  return h;
}
function cleanInterests(v){ if(!v) return 'Not Provided';
  let i=String(v);
  i=i.replace(/halloween orgy/gi,'Halloween');
  i=i.replace(/frying oil/gi,'').replace(/,\s*,/g,',').replace(/^\s*,|,\s*$/g,'');
  return i.trim();
}
function standardizeMusicPreference(m){ if(!m) return 'Not Provided'; const s=String(m).toLowerCase();
  if(s.includes('indie')||s.includes('alt')) return 'Indie/Alt';
  if(s==='pop') return 'Pop';
  if(s.includes('hip')) return 'Hip-hop';
  if(s.includes('r&b')) return 'R&B';
  if(s==='rock') return 'Rock';
  if(s==='metal') return 'Metal';
  if(s.includes('elec')) return 'Electronic';
  if(s.includes('country')) return 'Country';
  if(s.includes('reggae')) return 'Reggaeton';
  if(s.includes('prog')) return 'Prog Rock';
  if(s.includes('amb')) return 'Ambient';
  if(s.includes('emo')) return 'Emo';
  if(s.includes('mix')||s.includes('all')||s.includes('every')) return 'Mixed / All Genres';
  return m;
}
function standardizePurchase(p){ if(!p) return 'Not Provided'; const s=String(p).toLowerCase();
  if(s.includes('tech')||s.includes('gadget')) return 'Tech gadget';
  if(s.includes('fashion')||s.includes('cloth')) return 'Fashion/Clothing';
  if(s.includes('home')||s.includes('kitchen')) return 'Home/Kitchen';
  if(s.includes('pet')) return 'Pet item';
  if(s.includes('fit')||s.includes('gear')) return 'Fitness gear';
  if(s.includes('course')||s.includes('app')) return 'Course/App';
  if(s.includes('car')||s.includes('motor')) return 'Car/Motorcycle';
  return p;
}
function standardizeWorstTrait(t){ if(!t) return 'Not Provided'; const s=String(t).toLowerCase();
  if(s.includes('anx')) return 'Anxious';
  if(s.includes('crit')) return 'Overly critical';
  if(s.includes('stub')) return 'Stubborn';
  if(s.includes('impul')) return 'Impulsive';
  if(s.includes('reck')) return 'Reckless';
  if(s.includes('guard')) return 'Guarded';
  if(s.includes('jeal')) return 'Jealous';
  if(s.includes('self-con')) return 'Self-conscious';
  if(s.includes('insec')) return 'Insecure';
  if(s.includes('distr')) return 'Distracted';
  return t;
}
function cleanSocialStance(v){ if(v===null||v===undefined||v==='') return 'Not Provided';
  const n=parseInt(v,10); return (!isNaN(n)&&n>=1&&n<=5)? n : v;
}

// optional dictionary loader (UID -> Screen Name)
function loadScreenNameDict_(ss){
  const map = {};
  const sh = ss.getSheetByName(DICT_SHEET);
  if(!sh) return map;
  const vals = sh.getDataRange().getValues();
  // expects 2 columns: ScreenName | UID (based on your sample)
  for(let i=1;i<vals.length;i++){
    const sn = String(vals[i][0]||'').trim();
    const uid= String(vals[i][1]||'').trim();
    if(sn && uid) map[uid] = sn;
  }
  return map;
}

<!DOCTYPE html>
<html>
<head>
  <base target="_top">
  <meta name="viewport" content="width=device-width, initial-scale=1.0">
  <title>Guest Check-In</title>
  <style>
    * {
      margin: 0;
      padding: 0;
      box-sizing: border-box;
    }

<body>
  <div class="container">
    <h1>üéâ Guest Check-In</h1>
    <p class="subtitle">Please verify your identity to check in</p>
    
    <div id="message" class="message"></div>
    <div id="spinner" class="spinner"></div>
    
    <!-- Check-In Form -->
    <form id="checkInForm">
      <div class="form-group">
        <label for="zip">ZIP Code</label>
        <input type="text" id="zip" name="zip" placeholder="12345" maxlength="5" required>
        <div class="help-text">Enter your 5-digit ZIP code</div>
      </div>
      
      <div class="form-group">
        <label for="gender">Gender</label>
        <select id="gender" name="gender" required>
          <option value="">Select your gender</option>
          <option value="man">Man</option>
          <option value="woman">Woman</option>
          <option value="nonbinary">Non-binary</option>
          <option value="other">Other</option>
        </select>
      </div>
      
      <div class="form-group">
        <label for="dob">Birthday (MM/DD)</label>
        <input type="text" id="dob" name="dob" placeholder="03/15" maxlength="5" required>
        <div class="help-text">Format: MM/DD (e.g., 03/15)</div>
      </div>
      
      <button type="submit" class="btn" id="checkInBtn">Check In</button>
    </form>
    
    <!-- Guest Info (shown after check-in) -->
    <div id="guestInfo" class="guest-info">
      <h2>‚úÖ Checked In!</h2>
      <div class="info-row">
        <span class="info-label">Screen Name:</span>
        <span class="info-value" id="screenName"></span>
      </div>
      <div class="info-row">
        <span class="info-label">UID:</span>
        <span class="info-value" id="uid"></span>
      </div>
      
      <!-- Screen Name Update Section -->
      <div class="screen-name-section" id="screenNameSection">
        <h3 style="margin-bottom: 10px; font-size: 16px;">Update Screen Name</h3>
        <div class="form-group">
          <input type="text" id="newScreenName" placeholder="Enter new screen name" maxlength="50">
          <div class="help-text">3-50 characters</div>
        </div>
        <button class="btn" id="updateNameBtn">Update Name</button>
      </div>
      
      <!-- Photo Upload Section -->
      <div class="photo-section">
        <h3 style="margin-bottom: 10px; font-size: 16px;">üì∏ Upload Your Photo</h3>
        <div class="file-input-wrapper">
          <input type="file" id="photoInput" accept="image/*" capture="environment">
          <label for="photoInput" class="file-label">
            üì∑ Take or Choose Photo
          </label>
        </div>
        <div id="photoPreview" class="photo-preview">
          <img id="previewImg" src="" alt="Preview">
        </div>

  <script>
    let currentGuest = null;
    
    // Check-In Form Handler
    document.getElementById('checkInForm').addEventListener('submit', function(e) {
      e.preventDefault();
      
      const zip = document.getElementById('zip').value.trim();
      const gender = document.getElementById('gender').value;
      const dob = document.getElementById('dob').value.trim();
      
      // Validate DOB format
      if (!dob.match(/^\d{1,2}\/\d{1,2}$/)) {
        showMessage('Please use MM/DD format for birthday (e.g., 03/15)', 'error');
        return;
      }
      
      showSpinner(true);
      showMessage('Checking you in...', 'info');
      
      // Call the backend function
      google.script.run
        .withSuccessHandler(onCheckInSuccess)
        .withFailureHandler(onCheckInError)
        .checkInGuest({zip: zip, gender: gender, dob: dob});
    });
    
    function onCheckInSuccess(result) {
      showSpinner(false);
      
      if (result.ok) {
        currentGuest = {
          screenName: result.screenName,
          uid: result.uid
        };
        
        document.getElementById('screenName').textContent = result.screenName;
        document.getElementById('uid').textContent = result.uid;
        
        if (result.alreadyCheckedIn) {
          showMessage(result.message + ' You can update your info or upload a photo.', 'info');
        } else {
          showMessage(result.message, 'success');
        }
        
        // Hide form, show guest info
        document.getElementById('checkInForm').style.display = 'none';
        document.getElementById('guestInfo').style.display = 'block';
        document.getElementById('screenNameSection').style.display = 'block';
      } else {
        showMessage(result.message || 'Check-in failed. Please try again.', 'error');
      }
    }
    
    function onCheckInError(error) {
      showSpinner(false);
      showMessage('Error: ' + error.message, 'error');
      console.error('Check-in error:', error);
    }
    
    // Screen Name Update Handler
    document.getElementById('updateNameBtn').addEventListener('click', function() {
      const newName = document.getElementById('newScreenName').value.trim();
      
      if (!newName) {
        showMessage('Please enter a new screen name', 'error');
        return;
      }
      
      if (newName.length < 3) {
        showMessage('Screen name must be at least 3 characters', 'error');
        return;
      }
      
      showSpinner(true);
      showMessage('Updating screen name...', 'info');
      
      google.script.run
        .withSuccessHandler(onNameUpdateSuccess)
        .withFailureHandler(onNameUpdateError)
        .updateGuestScreenName({uid: currentGuest.uid, newScreenName: newName});
    });
    
    function onNameUpdateSuccess(result) {
      showSpinner(false);
      
      if (result.ok) {
        showMessage(result.message, 'success');
        document.getElementById('screenName').textContent = result.newScreenName;
        currentGuest.screenName = result.newScreenName;
        document.getElementById('newScreenName').value = '';
      } else {
        showMessage(result.message, 'error');
      }
    }
    
    function onNameUpdateError(error) {
      showSpinner(false);
      showMessage('Error updating name: ' + error.message, 'error');
    }
    
    // Photo Input Handler
    document.getElementById('photoInput').addEventListener('change', function(e) {
      const file = e.target.files[0];
      if (!file) return;
      
      // Validate file type
      if (!file.type.startsWith('image/')) {
        showMessage('Please select an image file', 'error');
        return;
      }
      
      // Validate file size (max 10MB)
      if (file.size > 10 * 1024 * 1024) {
        showMessage('Image must be smaller than 10MB', 'error');
        return;
      }
      
      // Show preview
      const reader = new FileReader();
      reader.onload = function(e) {
        document.getElementById('previewImg').src = e.target.result;
        document.getElementById('photoPreview').style.display = 'block';
        document.getElementById('uploadPhotoBtn').style.display = 'block';
      };
      reader.readAsDataURL(file);
    });
    
    // Photo Upload Handler
    document.getElementById('uploadPhotoBtn').addEventListener('click', function() {
      const fileInput = document.getElementById('photoInput');
      const file = fileInput.files[0];
      
      if (!file) {
        showMessage('Please select a photo first', 'error');
        return;
      }
      
      showSpinner(true);
      showMessage('Uploading photo...', 'info');
      
      const reader = new FileReader();
      reader.onload = function(e) {
        const base64Data = e.target.result.split(',')[1]; // Remove data:image/...;base64, prefix
        
        google.script.run
          .withSuccessHandler(onPhotoUploadSuccess)
          .withFailureHandler(onPhotoUploadError)
          .uploadGuestPhoto({
            uid: currentGuest.uid,
            fileName: file.name,
            mimeType: file.type,
            base64Data: base64Data
          });
      };
      reader.readAsDataURL(file);
    });
    
    function onPhotoUploadSuccess(result) {
      showSpinner(false);
      
      if (result.ok) {
        showMessage(result.message + ' ‚úÖ', 'success');
        document.getElementById('uploadPhotoBtn').style.display = 'none';
      } else {
        showMessage(result.message, 'error');
      }
    }
    
    function onPhotoUploadError(error) {
      showSpinner(false);
      showMessage('Error uploading photo: ' + error.message, 'error');
    }
    
    // Utility Functions
    function showMessage(text, type) {
      const msgDiv = document.getElementById('message');
      msgDiv.textContent = text;
      msgDiv.className = 'message ' + type;
      msgDiv.style.display = 'block';
    }
    
    function showSpinner(show) {
      document.getElementById('spinner').style.display = show ? 'block' : 'none';
    }
  </script>
</body>
</html>
ChatGPT said:

Thought for 7s
Here‚Äôs a hardened, cleaned version of your check-in page. I fixed validation, race conditions (double-submit), accessibility, and error handling; added safer input patterns; guarded calls if google.script.run isn‚Äôt present; and tightened the photo flow. Drop this in as a full replacement.

What I changed (high level)
Strict patterns for ZIP and birthday; mobile‚Äêfriendly inputmode.

Disabled submit while processing; prevents double check-ins.

Graceful fallback if google.script.run is unavailable (local preview won‚Äôt explode).

Better error surfacing and reset states; consistent success/error message handling.

Accessible labels/roles; keyboard/enter submits; focus management.

Photo size/type checks, preview reset, and upload button state logic.

Safer base64 extraction; guards against empty uid.

Minor CSS polish and consistent component spacing.

  <script>
    (function(){
      const $ = sel => document.querySelector(sel);
      const msg = $('#message');
      const spinner = $('#spinner');
      const form = $('#checkInForm');
      const btnCheckIn = $('#checkInBtn');
      const inputZip = $('#zip');
      const inputGender = $('#gender');
      const inputDob = $('#dob');
      const hp = $('#website'); // honeypot

      const guestInfo = $('#guestInfo');
      const screenNameEl = $('#screenName');
      const uidEl = $('#uid');
      const snSection = $('#screenNameSection');
      const btnUpdateName = $('#updateNameBtn');
      const inputNewSN = $('#newScreenName');

      const photoInput = $('#photoInput');
      const photoPreview = $('#photoPreview');
      const previewImg = $('#previewImg');
      const btnUpload = $('#uploadPhotoBtn');

      let currentGuest = null;
      let busy = false;

      function showMessage(text, type='info'){
        msg.textContent = text;
        msg.className = 'message ' + type;
        msg.style.display = 'block';
      }
      function clearMessage(){ msg.textContent=''; msg.style.display='none'; }
      function setBusy(on){
        busy = !!on;
        spinner.style.display = on ? 'block' : 'none';
        btnCheckIn.disabled = on;
        btnUpdateName.disabled = on;
        btnUpload.disabled = on;
      }
      function focusFirstInvalid(){
        const invalid = form.querySelector(':invalid');
        if (invalid) invalid.focus();
      }
      function gasAvailable(){
        return typeof google !== 'undefined' && google.script && google.script.run;
      }

      // Validate helpers
      function validZip(v){ return /^\d{5}$/.test(v); }
      function validDob(v){ return /^(0[1-9]|1[0-2])\/(0[1-9]|[12]\d|3[01])$/.test(v); }
      function sanitize(str){ return String(str || '').trim(); }

      // Submit handler
      form.addEventListener('submit', function(e){
        e.preventDefault();
        if (busy) return;

        // Honeypot check
        if (hp && sanitize(hp.value) !== '') {
          // Silent drop: bot likely
          return;
        }

        const zip = sanitize(inputZip.value);
        const gender = sanitize(inputGender.value);
        const dob = sanitize(inputDob.value);

        if (!validZip(zip)) { showMessage('ZIP must be 5 digits.', 'error'); inputZip.focus(); return; }
        if (!gender) { showMessage('Please select your gender.', 'error'); inputGender.focus(); return; }
        if (!validDob(dob)) { showMessage('Use MM/DD format for birthday (e.g., 03/15).', 'error'); inputDob.focus(); return; }

        setBusy(true);
        showMessage('Checking you in...', 'info');

        const payload = { zip, gender, dob };

        if (!gasAvailable()) {
          // Local preview fallback
          setTimeout(() => {
            setBusy(false);
            const fake = { ok:true, alreadyCheckedIn:false, screenName:'Guest_000', uid:'UID_DEMO', message:'(Preview) Check-in ok.' };
            onCheckInSuccess(fake);
          }, 600);
          return;
        }

        google.script.run
          .withSuccessHandler(onCheckInSuccess)
          .withFailureHandler(onCheckInError)
          .checkInGuest(payload);
      });

      function onCheckInSuccess(result){
        setBusy(false);
        if (!result || !result.ok) {
          showMessage((result && result.message) || 'Check-in failed. Try again.', 'error');
          return;
        }
        currentGuest = { screenName: result.screenName, uid: result.uid };

        screenNameEl.textContent = result.screenName || '‚Äî';
        uidEl.textContent = result.uid || '‚Äî';

        showMessage(result.message + (result.alreadyCheckedIn ? ' You can update your info or upload a photo.' : ''), result.alreadyCheckedIn ? 'info' : 'success');

        form.style.display = 'none';
        guestInfo.style.display = 'block';
        snSection.style.display = 'block';

        // Focus the screen name input for quick edit
        inputNewSN.focus();
      }
      function onCheckInError(error){
        setBusy(false);
        const msgText = (error && (error.message || error.toString())) || 'Unknown error.';
        showMessage('Error during check-in: ' + msgText, 'error');
        console.error('Check-in error:', error);
      }

      // Update screen name
      btnUpdateName.addEventListener('click', function(){
        if (busy) return;
        if (!currentGuest || !currentGuest.uid) { showMessage('No active guest session.', 'error'); return; }

        const newName = sanitize(inputNewSN.value);
        if (newName.length < 3) { showMessage('Screen name must be at least 3 characters.', 'error'); inputNewSN.focus(); return; }
        if (newName.length > 50) { showMessage('Screen name must be 50 characters or fewer.', 'error'); inputNewSN.focus(); return; }

        setBusy(true);
        showMessage('Updating screen name...', 'info');

        if (!gasAvailable()) {
          setTimeout(() => {
            setBusy(false);
            screenNameEl.textContent = newName;
            currentGuest.screenName = newName;
            inputNewSN.value = '';
            showMessage('(Preview) Screen name updated.', 'success');
          }, 400);
          return;
        }

        google.script.run
          .withSuccessHandler(onNameUpdateSuccess)
          .withFailureHandler(onNameUpdateError)
          .updateGuestScreenName({ uid: currentGuest.uid, newScreenName: newName });
      });

      function onNameUpdateSuccess(result){
        setBusy(false);
        if (!result || !result.ok) { showMessage((result && result.message) || 'Update failed.', 'error'); return; }
        screenNameEl.textContent = result.newScreenName || screenNameEl.textContent;
        if (currentGuest) currentGuest.screenName = result.newScreenName;
        inputNewSN.value = '';
        showMessage(result.message || 'Screen name updated.', 'success');
      }
      function onNameUpdateError(error){
        setBusy(false);
        showMessage('Error updating name: ' + (error && (error.message || error.toString())), 'error');
      }

      // Photo selection
      photoInput.addEventListener('change', function(e){
        clearMessage();
        const file = e.target.files && e.target.files[0];
        if (!file) return;

        if (!file.type || !file.type.startsWith('image/')) {
          showMessage('Please select an image file.', 'error'); resetPhotoPreview(); return;
        }
        if (file.size > 10 * 1024 * 1024) {
          showMessage('Image must be smaller than 10MB.', 'error'); resetPhotoPreview(); return;
        }

        const reader = new FileReader();
        reader.onload = function(ev){
          previewImg.src = ev.target.result;
          photoPreview.style.display = 'block';
          btnUpload.style.display = 'block';
        };
        reader.onerror = function(){ showMessage('Could not read the image file.', 'error'); resetPhotoPreview(); };
        reader.readAsDataURL(file);
      });

      function resetPhotoPreview(){
        previewImg.src = '';
        photoPreview.style.display = 'none';
        btnUpload.style.display = 'none';
        photoInput.value = '';
      }

      // Photo upload
      btnUpload.addEventListener('click', function(){
        if (busy) return;
        if (!currentGuest || !currentGuest.uid) { showMessage('No active guest session.', 'error'); return; }

        const file = photoInput.files && photoInput.files[0];
        if (!file) { showMessage('Please select a photo first.', 'error'); return; }

        setBusy(true);
        showMessage('Uploading photo...', 'info');

        const reader = new FileReader();
        reader.onload = function(ev){
          const dataUrl = ev.target.result || '';
          const parts = dataUrl.split(',');
          if (parts.length < 2) {
            setBusy(false);
            showMessage('Invalid image data.', 'error');
            return;
          }
          const base64Data = parts[1];

          if (!gasAvailable()) {
            setBusy(false);
            showMessage('(Preview) Photo upload ok.', 'success');
            btnUpload.style.display = 'none';
            return;
          }

          google.script.run
            .withSuccessHandler(onPhotoUploadSuccess)
            .withFailureHandler(onPhotoUploadError)
            .uploadGuestPhoto({
              uid: currentGuest.uid,
              fileName: file.name,
              mimeType: file.type || 'image/jpeg',
              base64Data: base64Data
            });
        };
        reader.onerror = function(){
          setBusy(false);
          showMessage('Error reading image.', 'error');
        };
        reader.readAsDataURL(file);
      });

      function onPhotoUploadSuccess(result){
        setBusy(false);
        if (!result || !result.ok) {
          showMessage((result && result.message) || 'Upload failed.', 'error');
          return;
        }
        showMessage(result.message + ' ‚úÖ', 'success');
        btnUpload.style.display = 'none';
      }
      function onPhotoUploadError(error){
        setBusy(false);
        showMessage('Error uploading photo: ' + (error && (error.message || error.toString())), 'error');
      }

      // Convenience: Enter key in inputs submits
      ['zip','gender','dob'].forEach(id => {
        const el = document.getElementById(id);
        el && el.addEventListener('keydown', (ev) => {
          if (ev.key === 'Enter' && !busy) form.requestSubmit();
        });
      });
    })();
  </script>
</body>
</html>
If you want, I‚Äôll also give you minimal backend stubs for checkInGuest, updateGuestScreenName, and uploadGuestPhoto that match this client‚Äôs payloads and return shapes‚Äîso you can drop them into Apps Script without guesswork.

ChatGPT said:
Here‚Äôs a tight, production-ready analytics spec for your Panopticon (system view) and Compatibility Wall (pairwise view). It splits into three artifacts you named, with concrete fields, formulas, and outputs. You can implement this directly in Apps Script or Sheets formulas.

1) Pan_Master (one row per guest; all calculated fields)
Purpose: single source of truth for every visualization: terminal, compatibility, and map.

1.1 Columns (inputs carry over; everything else is derived)
Identity & hygiene

UID (key)

ScreenName

CheckedIn (bool), CheckInTime

PhotoURL

RowStatus (OK | Missing_Zip | Missing_Interests | etc.)

Demographics (as in clean sheet)

AgeRange, Gender, Ethnicity, Orientation, Education

Birthday, Zodiac

Zip5, Lat, Lng (zip centroid; leave blank if unknown)

Social / host

KnowHosts (enum), KnownLongest (Jacob/Michael/Equal/Unknown)

KnowStrength (1‚Äì5)

SocialStance (1‚Äì5)

Interests & culture

Interests[] (array, ‚â§5 items; normalized)

MusicGenre (bucketed), FavArtist, SongRequest

WorstTrait (normalized set)

Panopticon metrics

Polarity_Stability ‚àà [-1, +1]
Map worst trait ‚Üí numeric:
Impulsive=+0.8, Reckless=+0.8, Distracted=+0.6, Stubborn=+0.4, Jealous=+0.3,
Self-conscious=-0.4, Insecure=-0.5, Guarded=-0.6, Anxious=-0.6, Overly critical=-0.3

Polarity_Openness ‚àà [-1, +1]
Example mapping: Impulsive=+0.7, Reckless=+0.6, Distracted=+0.3, Stubborn=-0.2, Jealous=-0.3,
Anxious=-0.5, Guarded=-0.7, Insecure=-0.6, Self-conscious=-0.5, Overly critical=-0.4

HostGroup (Jacob/Michael/Equal/Unknown)

Cohort (AgeRange bucket as numeric order: 21‚Äì24=1 ‚Ä¶ 55‚Äì65+=6)

TravelMiles (great-circle distance to venue; blank if no lat/lng)

Completeness (0‚Äì1)
= mean of presence flags across: Interests, MusicGenre, AgeRange, Zip5, WorstTrait, SocialStance, Zodiac.

Compatibility primitives (to reuse across pages)

InterestsKey (sorted, comma-joined interests)

GenreKey (single bucket)

ZodiacKey (12-sign enum)

StanceKey (= SocialStance int)

AgeKey (Cohort int)

IndustryRoleKey (e.g., Industry|Role)

Recommended visuals hooks

NodeSize (map to AgeKey or Completeness)

NodeShape (HostGroup)

NodeJitter (|Polarity_Openness| * 0.8)

NodeHue (MusicGenre ‚Üí deterministic hue)

2) V_Cramer_Cat (Cram√©r‚Äôs V between categorical variables)
Purpose: quantify associations across variables for control of your storytelling and algorithm weights.

2.1 Variables to include
Demographics: AgeRange, Gender, Ethnicity, Orientation, Education, Zodiac

Culture: MusicGenre, Interests (explode to one-hot across the top ~20 most common tags)

Social: HostGroup, KnowStrength (bin 1‚Äì2, 3, 4‚Äì5), SocialStance (bin 1‚Äì2, 3, 4‚Äì5)

Location: Zip5 (coarsen to first 3 digits Zip3 to reduce sparsity)

2.2 Output tables
V_Matrix (wide table)

Rows: variable A; Cols: variable B; Cell = Cram√©r‚Äôs V (0‚Äì1).

Compute on checked-in only. Suppress cells where any category has <5 counts (reduce instability).

Flag cells with p < 0.05 using chi-square with Yates correction (optional).

Top_Associations (long table)

Columns: VarA, VarB, V, pValue, N, Note

Keep top 20 V values where N ‚â• 50.

Cluster assignments (guest-level)

Clustering options (pick at least one):

K-modes or K-prototypes on categorical vectors (Interests one-hot + Music + Zodiac + HostGroup + Stance bin).

Agglomerative on Hamming distance.

For Sheets-native: compute Jaccard similarity on Interests and then do spectral clustering with 2‚Äì4 clusters (Apps Script).

Output: UID, ClusterId_{method}, Silhouette_{method}.

2.3 How to compute Cram√©r‚Äôs V (reference)
For each pair (A,B), build contingency table.

œá¬≤ from the table; n = total count; k = min(#levels(A), #levels(B))

V = sqrt( œá¬≤ / ( n * (k - 1) ) )

For sparse tables, collapse rare categories into Other.

Usage:

Use V to weight features in similarity (e.g., if Music‚ÜîInterests V is high, slightly down-weight one to avoid double counting).

3) Guest Similarity Score (pairwise; used in Compatibility Wall)
Purpose: produce both similar and complementary matches. You‚Äôll compute two scores and surface both.

3.1 Feature set (balanced, defensible)
High-signal: Interests[], MusicGenre

Medium: AgeRange adjacency, SocialStance proximity

Contextual: HostGroup overlap (shared community), Zodiac compatibility (lightweight), IndustryRole (weak)

3.2 Similarity score (0‚Äì100)
Sim(A,B) =
  0.45 * Jaccard(InterestsA, InterestsB)
+ 0.20 * GenreMatch(MusicA, MusicB)         // 1 exact, 0.5 close, 0 otherwise
+ 0.10 * AgeAdj(AgeKeyA, AgeKeyB)           // 1 same, 0.5 adjacent (¬±1), else 0
+ 0.10 * StanceProx(|StanceA - StanceB|)    // 1 if diff ‚â§0, 0.75 if 1, 0.5 if 2, 0.25 if 3, 0 if 4+
+ 0.10 * HostProx(HostGroupA, HostGroupB, min(KnowStrengthA,KnowStrengthB))
+ 0.05 * IndRoleMatch(IndustryRoleA, IndustryRoleB)  // 1 exact, 0.5 same industry, else 0
Scale: multiply by 100 and round to integer.

Genre closeness map (examples):

Pop ‚Üî R&B (0.5), Pop ‚Üî Electronic (0.5), Indie/Alt ‚Üî Rock (0.5), Hip-hop ‚Üî R&B (0.5), Prog Rock ‚Üî Rock (0.5), Metal ‚Üî Rock (0.5). Others 0.

HostProx: 1 if same HostGroup and both KnowStrength ‚â• 4; 0.5 if same HostGroup; else 0.

Edge rule for graph: show edges where Sim ‚â• 45. Cap to top-5 neighbors per node to avoid hairballs.

3.3 Complementarity score (0‚Äì100)
Goal: pair people who ‚Äúcomplete‚Äù each other (polarity/openness complements) while keeping a minimum cultural overlap.

Comp(A,B) =
  0.30 * Oppose(Polarity_StabilityA, Polarity_StabilityB) // higher when signs differ
+ 0.20 * Oppose(Polarity_OpennessA,  Polarity_OpennessB)
+ 0.25 * Jaccard(InterestsA, InterestsB)                   // require a bridge
+ 0.10 * GenreMatch(MusicA, MusicB)
+ 0.10 * StanceBalance(StanceA, StanceB)                   // highest near center spread (e.g., 2 vs 4)
+ 0.05 * ZodiacCompat(ZodiacA, ZodiacB)                    // simple 0/0.5/1
Oppose(x,y) = 1 - |x - y|/2 if x*y < 0 else 0.5 - |x - y|/2 (reward opposite signs; damp same-side).

StanceBalance peaks when average is ~3 with spread 1‚Äì2.

Guardrail: only consider complementary pairs if Jaccard(Interests) ‚â• 0.2 or GenreMatch ‚â• 0.5. Otherwise return 0 (too alien).

3.4 Outputs you should materialize
Pairwise table (for export and heatmap):
UID_A, UID_B, SimScore, CompScore, SharedInterestsCSV, MusicPair, AgeAdj, StanceDiff, ZodiacPair, HostPair, Flags

Flags examples: LowData (Completeness < 0.6), NoZip, SparseInterests.

Per-guest rollups (feed UI quickly):

TopSimilar[10] = list of {UID, Score, Why}

TopComplementary[10] = list of {UID, Score, Why}

Why = short template text:

Similar: ‚Äú{k} shared interests; {genre note}; {age note}‚Äù

Complementary: ‚ÄúOpposing polarity (+/-), shared {interest}, {stance note}‚Äù

Clustering (for the Panopticon view)
Use Interests one-hot + MusicGenre + Stance bin + HostGroup.

Method 1 (lightweight, Script-friendly): Agglomerative with Jaccard/Hamming; set k=3‚Äì5; compute silhouette.

Method 2 (if you add Node): K-prototypes (mix cat + binary).

Store: ClusterId, ClusterName (label by top interests), Silhouette.

Why clustering? It gives you scene segments for the theatre: highlight one cluster at a time during the ‚ÄúAnalyzing ‚Äî Interests/Music‚Äù cycle.

Travel / Map analytics
Venue lat/lng constant; compute great-circle miles.

Store distribution: counts per bin [0‚Äì5, 5‚Äì10, 10‚Äì25, 25‚Äì50, 50‚Äì100, 100+].

Summary: MedianMiles, P90Miles.

Add Zip3 choropleth counts for regional view.

Governance & privacy
Keep names out of analytics tables (ScreenName is okay for display; don‚Äôt export real names).

Jitter map points by ¬±0.5‚Äì1 km.

Don‚Äôt compute pairwise scores for guests with Completeness < 0.4.

Limit any public export to UID and abstract attributes only.

Implementation notes (Sheet / Script quick wins)
Jaccard(Interests): split to sets by comma, lowercase/trim; |‚à©|/|‚à™|. Cache per UID pair.

AgeAdj: if |AgeKeyA ‚àí AgeKeyB| == 0 ‚Üí 1; ==1 ‚Üí 0.5; else 0.

StanceProx: map diff 0‚Üí1, 1‚Üí0.75, 2‚Üí0.5, 3‚Üí0.25, ‚â•4‚Üí0.

ZodiacCompat: simple 12√ó12 lookup (High=1 for trines/oppositions, Medium=0.5 for sextiles, else 0).

Materialize Pan_Master first; all other artifacts read from it.

What you‚Äôll see in the UI (hooks)
Panopticon: node size = Completeness or AgeKey; jitter = |Polarity_Openness|; edge pulses keyed to the trait being analyzed; cluster toggle.

Compatibility Wall: tabs for Similar and Complementary; heatmap sorted by cluster; ‚ÄúWhy this match‚Äù tooltips use the rollups.

If you want, I‚Äôll generate:

a Pan_Master schema as a header row you can paste into a new sheet, and

an Apps Script scorer that fills Sim/Comp pairwise tables with the exact formulas above.

Thought for 8s
Direct and simple:

What goes where (and why)
A) Compatibility (matching people to people)
Use these features ‚Äî only. They‚Äôre behaviorally relevant and low-risk for bias.

Interests: Interest_1..3 (normalize to a small taxonomy; use Jaccard).

Music Preference: Music Preference (map to 8‚Äì10 buckets; keep a genre-proximity table).

Social vibe: Which best describes your general social stance? (1‚Äì5; use proximity).

Age adjacency: Age Range (cohort difference 0 or ¬±1 only; don‚Äôt hard-prefer exact ages).

Host community: Do you know the Host(s)?, Which host‚Ä¶, If yes, how well‚Ä¶ (use only for soft ties / reducing cold introductions).

Zodiac Sign: optional flavor (0/0.5/1 lookup).

Travel/Zip (very light): use distance only to de-prioritize ultra-distant pairs if you‚Äôre suggesting immediate in-person intros.

Do NOT use for matching (to avoid discriminatory or creepy outcomes):

Self Identified Ethnicity, Self-Identified Gender, Self-Identified Sexual Orientation, Education Level, Employment‚Ä¶ (Industry/Role).
Keep these out of the scoring. If you ever look at them, do it only to audit for skew.

Practical scoring recipe (0‚Äì100) ‚Äî production-ready weights:

0.45 * Jaccard(Interests)

0.20 * GenreMatch (1 exact; 0.5 close; else 0)

0.10 * AgeAdj (1 same cohort; 0.5 adjacent; else 0)

0.10 * StanceProx (diff 0‚Üí1; 1‚Üí0.75; 2‚Üí0.5; 3‚Üí0.25; ‚â•4‚Üí0)

0.10 * HostProx (1 same host & both know ‚â•4; 0.5 same host; else 0)

0.05 * IndRoleMatch (optional: 1 same role; 0.5 same industry; else 0) ‚Äî default OFF to avoid occupational clustering unless you explicitly want it.

Guardrails

Exclude rows with DDD_Score < 2 or missing Interest_* from pair scoring.

Edge display threshold: only show pairs with score ‚â• 45, cap to top-5 neighbors per guest.

B) Marketing demographics & reporting (segment people to audiences)
Use these for segmentation dashboards, not for person-to-person matching:

Core demo: Age Range, Education Level (bin), Current 5 Digit Zip Code ‚Üí Zip3 (or City), Employment Industry (10‚Äì12 buckets), Employment Role (8‚Äì10 buckets).

Culture: Music Preference (bucket), Top interests (collapsed to 15‚Äì20 tags max).

Community: host familiarity (Do you know‚Ä¶, Which host‚Ä¶, How well‚Ä¶).

Engagement: Checked-In (Y/N), Check-in Time (recency), Song request (Y/N), Photo URL present (Y/N).

Travel: compute TravelMiles from Zip5 to venue (then bin: 0‚Äì5, 5‚Äì10, 10‚Äì25, 25‚Äì50, 50‚Äì100, 100+).

Keep sensitive attributes out of targeting logic (or use only for aggregate heatmaps / fairness audits):

Self Identified Ethnicity, Self-Identified Gender, Self-Identified Sexual Orientation.
Report distribution; do not drive outreach or offers with them.

KPIs to ship

Attendance funnel by cohort (21‚Äì24, 25‚Äì29, 30‚Äì34, 35‚Äì44, 55‚Äì65+).

Genre mix, Top-10 interests penetration.

New vs returning (by host familiarity), Median & P90 TravelMiles.

Engagement: % with song requests, % with photos, check-in curve over time.

C) Algorithm plumbing / feature engineering (both sides share these primitives)
Canonical bins / keys
AgeKey: 21‚Äì24=1, 25‚Äì29=2, 30‚Äì34=3, 35‚Äì44=4, 55‚Äì65+=5.

Zip3: first 3 digits of Zip5.

GenreKey: map raw to one of: Pop, R&B, Hip-hop, Electronic, Indie/Alt, Rock, Metal, Country, Prog Rock, Ambient, Emo, Mixed/All.

InterestsKey: lowercase, trimmed, deduped; restrict the dictionary to ~20 (e.g., music, fitness, gaming, cooking, reading, hiking, travel, art/design, fashion, photography, sports, film/movies, volunteering, dancing, health sciences, cars, TikTok, politics, pet, home/kitchen).

StanceKey: the 1‚Äì5 integer.

HostGroup: Jacob, Michael, Equal, Unknown.

Data quality / gating
DDD_Score (you already have it; treat as ‚Äúdata depth/density‚Äù).

Low (<2): allow in marketing aggregates; exclude from pair scoring.

Med (2‚Äì4): allow; reduce match weight 10%.

High (‚â•5): full weight.

Optional psych hooks (for complementary matching only)
WorstTrait ‚Üí Polarity vectors

Stability ‚àà [-1, +1] and Openness ‚àà [-1, +1] via a lookup (as defined earlier).

Use only for the Complementary tab, never for ‚Äúsimilar.‚Äù

Field-by-field routing (cheat sheet)
Column	Compatibility	Marketing/Reporting	Notes

Concrete groupings to implement
Genres (proximity table examples)

Exact match = 1.0

Close = 0.5: Pop‚ÜîR&B, Pop‚ÜîElectronic, Indie/Alt‚ÜîRock, Hip-hop‚ÜîR&B, Prog Rock‚ÜîRock, Metal‚ÜîRock.

Else 0.0

Interest taxonomy (cap at ~20)
music, fitness, gaming, cooking, reading, hiking/outdoors, travel, art/design, fashion, photography, sports, film/movies, volunteering, dancing, health sciences, cars, tiktok, politics, pet, home/kitchen.
‚Üí Map odd inputs (‚ÄúHalloween orgy‚Äù, ‚Äúfrying oil‚Äù) to safe parents or drop.

Education bins (for reporting)
High School, Associates, Some College, Bachelors, Masters+.

Role bins (see table above).

Zip ‚Üí location

Zip3 = LEFT(Zip5, 3)

TravelMiles = Haversine(ZipCentroid, Venue); bin as suggested.

Minimal scoring pseudo (Apps Script)
// Jaccard on 3 normalized interests per guest
function jaccard(a, b) {
  const A = new Set(a.filter(Boolean).map(s=>s.toLowerCase()));
  const B = new Set(b.filter(Boolean).map(s=>s.toLowerCase()));
  const inter = [...A].filter(x => B.has(x)).length;
  const uni = new Set([...A, ...B]).size;
  return uni ? inter/uni : 0;
}

function genreMatch(gA, gB){
  if (!gA || !gB) return 0;
  if (gA === gB) return 1;
  const close = new Set([['Pop','R&B'],['Pop','Electronic'],['Indie/Alt','Rock'],
                         ['Hip-hop','R&B'],['Prog Rock','Rock'],['Metal','Rock']]
                        .map(([x,y])=>x+'|'+y));
  return (close.has(gA+'|'+gB') || close.has(gB+'|'+gA)) ? 0.5 : 0;
}

function ageAdj(a, b){ const d = Math.abs(a-b); return d===0?1 : d===1?0.5 : 0; }

function stanceProx(a, b){
  const d = Math.abs((a|0) - (b|0));
  return d===0?1 : d===1?0.75 : d===2?0.5 : d===3?0.25 : 0;
}

function hostProx(hA, hB, sA, sB){
  if (hA && hA===hB) return (Math.min(+sA||0, +sB||0) >= 4) ? 1 : 0.5;
  return 0;
}

function simScore(rowA, rowB){
  // ageKey is cohort int; interests is [Interest_1..3]; genreKey is normalized genre string
  const w = {jac:0.45, gen:0.20, age:0.10, stance:0.10, host:0.10, ind:0.05};
  const s =
    w.jac  * jaccard(rowA.interests, rowB.interests) +
    w.gen  * genreMatch(rowA.genreKey, rowB.genreKey) +
    w.age  * ageAdj(rowA.ageKey, rowB.ageKey) +
    w.stance * stanceProx(rowA.stance, rowB.stance) +
    w.host * hostProx(rowA.hostGroup, rowB.hostGroup, rowA.knowStrength, rowB.knowStrength);
  return Math.round(s * 100);
}
Implementation order of operations
Normalize & gate: build Pan_Master with keys above; compute DDD_Score if missing; mark Checked-In.

Marketing views: cohort/genre/interest/zip3 distributions + travel bins + engagement.

Compatibility graph: compute pair scores only among checked-in & DDD‚â•2; render Similar and Complementary tabs; show ‚ÄúWhy this match‚Äù using shared interests + genre note + stance note.

Audit: monthly Cram√©r‚Äôs V across marketing fields to detect redundancy and to monitor for unintended correlations.

If you want, I‚Äôll turn this into:

a header template for Pan_Master,

a Sheets formula pack (including Haversine), and

a script that produces the pairwise table with the exact weights above.
